%%%

operation:

PROCEDURE

(v,
v)

(v.X*v.X
+
v.Y*v.Y
+
v.Z*v.Z
+
v.W*v.W)
%%%

cross

(v,
v)
RETURN
(v.Y*v.Z-v.Z*v
.Y,
v.Z*v.X-v.X*
v.Z,
v.X*v.Y-v.Y*v.X
)

v,
v)

(vdot(vcross(v,
v,
v))

(test

RETURN
NBR
